out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _ScaleOffset0.xy + _ScaleOffset0.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _ScaleOffset1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy + _ScaleOffset1.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

void main()
{

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;

    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = 0.0;

    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;

    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);

    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _Color0;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _ScaleOffset0;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Layer0Metaloffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Layer0Roughoffset;

UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _battlefogMap;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _ScaleOffset0.xy + _ScaleOffset0.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _ScaleOffset1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy + _ScaleOffset1.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD4.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _battlefogParam.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18 = textureLod(_battlefogMap, u_xlat1.xy, 0.0).y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.y / _battlefogCustomParam.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + (-_battlefogCustomParam.y);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * u_xlat18 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(abs(u_xlat18));
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _battlefogCustomParam.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xxxx);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.y / _battlefogCustomParam.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + (-_battlefogCustomParam.y);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * u_xlat18 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(abs(u_xlat18));
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _battlefogCustomParam.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xxxx);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap1, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.yyy;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap0, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.xxx + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-_battlefogColor.xyz) * _battlefogColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _battlefogColor.xyz * _battlefogColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.xyz + _battlefogCustomParam.zzz;

#else
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = clamp(u_xlat16_3.xyz, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _battlefogMap;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _ScaleOffset0.xy + _ScaleOffset0.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _ScaleOffset1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy + _ScaleOffset1.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4.w = u_xlat16_1.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat16_1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _battlefogParam.xy;
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat2.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18 = textureLod(_battlefogMap, u_xlat2.xy, 0.0).y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.y / _battlefogCustomParam.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + (-_battlefogCustomParam.y);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * u_xlat18 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(abs(u_xlat18));
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _battlefogCustomParam.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xxxx);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseMap0;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseMap1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
bool u_xlatb5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
void main()
{
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(vs_TEXCOORD7.xy,vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
    u_xlat16_0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb5 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb5 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb5 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap1, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.yyy;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap0, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.xxx + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHAr.yw, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHAg.yw, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHAb.yw, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + (-unity_SHC.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-_battlefogColor.xyz) * _battlefogColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _battlefogColor.xyz * _battlefogColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.xyz + _battlefogCustomParam.zzz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = clamp(u_xlat16_3.xyz, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;

UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _battlefogMap;

in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;

in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;

vec4 u_xlat0;

{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _ScaleOffset0.xy + _ScaleOffset0.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _ScaleOffset1.xy;

    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + (-_battlefogCustomParam.y);

    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);

vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _ScaleOffset0.xy + _ScaleOffset0.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _ScaleOffset1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy + _ScaleOffset1.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD4.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _battlefogParam.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18 = textureLod(_battlefogMap, u_xlat1.xy, 0.0).y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.y / _battlefogCustomParam.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + (-_battlefogCustomParam.y);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * u_xlat18 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(abs(u_xlat18));
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _battlefogCustomParam.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xxxx);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.454545468, 0.454545468, 0.454545468);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D unity_Lightmap;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseMap0;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseMap1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;

vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap1, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.yyy;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap0, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.xxx + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-_battlefogColor.xyz) * _battlefogColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _battlefogColor.xyz * _battlefogColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.xyz + _battlefogCustomParam.zzz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = clamp(u_xlat16_3.xyz, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.454545468, 0.454545468, 0.454545468);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _battlefogMap;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;

vec3 u_xlat4;

mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _ScaleOffset0.xy + _ScaleOffset0.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _ScaleOffset1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy + _ScaleOffset1.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4.w = u_xlat16_1.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat16_1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _battlefogParam.xy;
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat2.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18 = textureLod(_battlefogMap, u_xlat2.xy, 0.0).y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.y / _battlefogCustomParam.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + (-_battlefogCustomParam.y);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * u_xlat18 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(abs(u_xlat18));
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _battlefogCustomParam.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xxxx);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseMap0;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseMap1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
bool u_xlatb5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
void main()
{
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(vs_TEXCOORD7.xy,vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
    u_xlat16_0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb5 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb5 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb5 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap1, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.yyy;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseMap0, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _Color0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD2.xxx + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHAr.yw, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHAg.yw, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHAb.yw, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + (-unity_SHC.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-_battlefogColor.xyz) * _battlefogColor.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
